				<article class="elementor-post elementor-grid-item post-8317 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-php tag-data-types tag-php tag-variables" role="listitem">
			<div class="elementor-post__card">
				<a class="elementor-post__thumbnail__link" href="https://www.delightitsolutions.com/understanding-php-data-types-and-variables/" tabindex="-1"><div class="elementor-post__thumbnail"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="300" height="300" src="https://www.delightitsolutions.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/Understanding-PHP-Data-Types-and-Variables-300x300.jpg" class="attachment-medium size-medium wp-image-8846" alt="Understanding PHP Data Types and Variables" srcset="https://www.delightitsolutions.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/Understanding-PHP-Data-Types-and-Variables-300x300.jpg 300w, https://www.delightitsolutions.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/Understanding-PHP-Data-Types-and-Variables-150x150.jpg 150w, https://www.delightitsolutions.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/Understanding-PHP-Data-Types-and-Variables-320x320.jpg 320w, https://www.delightitsolutions.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/09/Understanding-PHP-Data-Types-and-Variables.jpg 512w" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" title="Blog Landing 152"></div></a>
				<div class="elementor-post__badge">Php</div>
				<div class="elementor-post__text">
				<h1 class="elementor-post__title">
			<a href="https://www.delightitsolutions.com/understanding-php-data-types-and-variables/">
				Understanding PHP Data Types and Variables			</a>
		</h1>
				<div class="elementor-post__excerpt">
			<p>PHP is a dynamically typed language, which means that variables do not have a fixed data type. The data type of a variable is determined</p>

					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];

					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
